SELECT a.name FROM ACCOUNTS a JOIN CHECKING c ON a.custid = c.custid JOIN SAVINGS s ON a.custid = s.custid WHERE c.balance > s.balance;
SELECT a.name FROM ACCOUNTS a JOIN CHECKING c ON a.custid = c.custid JOIN SAVINGS s ON a.custid = s.custid WHERE c.balance > s.balance;
SELECT a.name, SUM(s.balance) + SUM(c.balance) AS total_balance FROM ACCOUNTS a JOIN SAVINGS s ON a.custid = s.custid JOIN CHECKING c ON a.custid = c.custid WHERE s.balance < c.balance GROUP BY a.name;
SELECT A.name, SUM(C.balance) + SUM(S.balance) AS total_balance FROM ACCOUNTS A JOIN SAVINGS S ON A.custid = S.custid JOIN CHECKING C ON A.custid = C.custid WHERE S.balance < C.balance GROUP BY A.name;
SELECT A.name, S.balance FROM ACCOUNTS A JOIN SAVINGS S ON A.custid = S.custid ORDER BY S.balance DESC LIMIT 3;
SELECT a.name, s.balance FROM SAVINGS s JOIN ACCOUNTS a ON s.custid = a.custid ORDER BY s.balance DESC LIMIT 3;

SELECT     transportation_method,     COUNT(*) AS frequency FROM     (SELECT         'By Car' AS transportation_method         FROM             Visits v             JOIN Tourist_Attractions ta ON v.Tourist_Attraction_ID = ta.Tourist_Attraction_ID         WHERE             How_to_Get_There LIKE '%car%'     UNION ALL     SELECT         'By Public Transport' AS transportation_method         FROM             Visits v             JOIN Tourist_Attractions ta ON v.Tourist_Attraction_ID = ta.Tourist_Attraction_ID         WHERE             How_to_Get_There LIKE '%public%'     UNION ALL     SELECT         'On Foot' AS transportation_method         FROM             Visits v             JOIN Tourist_Attractions ta ON v.Tourist_Attraction_ID = ta.Tourist_Attraction_ID         WHERE             How_to_Get_There LIKE '%on foot%'     UNION ALL     SELECT         'By Bike' AS transportation_method         FROM             Visits v             JOIN Tourist_Attractions ta ON v.Tourist_Attraction_ID = ta.Tourist_Attraction_ID         WHERE             How_to_Get_There LIKE '%bike%'     UNION ALL     SELECT         'By Taxi' AS transportation_method         FROM             Visits v             JOIN Tourist_Attractions ta ON v.Tourist_Attraction_ID = ta.Tourist_Attraction_ID         WHERE             How_to_Get_There LIKE '%taxi%'     UNION ALL     SELECT         'Other' AS transportation_method         FROM             Visits v             JOIN Tourist_Attractions ta ON v.Tourist_Attraction_ID = ta.Tourist_Attraction_ID         WHERE             How_to_Get_There NOT LIKE '%car%'             AND How_to_Get_There NOT LIKE '%public%'             AND How_to_Get_There NOT LIKE '%on foot%'             AND How_to_Get_There NOT LIKE '%bike%'             AND How_to_Get_There NOT LIKE '%taxi%'     ) AS transportation_methods GROUP BY     transportation_method ORDER BY     frequency DESC;
